\f0\fs38 \cf2 \cb3 \strokec2 1. Gambaran Umum Sistem\cb1 \
\pard\pardeftab720\sa240\partightenfactor0

\fs32 \cf2 \cb3 PLTS SmartHome
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4  adalah sistem terintegrasi untuk monitoring dan kontrol Pembangkit Listrik Tenaga Surya (PLTS) yang dikombinasikan dengan fitur SmartHome. Sistem ini dirancang untuk rumah tinggal dengan kebutuhan energi yang didukung oleh panel surya dan baterai LiFePO4 8S.\cb1 \
\pard\pardeftab720\sa240\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \cb3 Sistem terdiri dari tiga komponen utama yang saling terhubung:\cb1 \
\pard\tx220\tx720\pardeftab720\li720\fi-720\sa160\partightenfactor0
\ls2\ilvl0
\f0 \cf2 \cb3 \kerning1\expnd0\expndtw0 \outl0\strokewidth0 {\listtext	1.	}\expnd0\expndtw0\kerning0
\outl0\strokewidth0 \strokec2 ESP32 Firmware
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4  \'97 Controller perangkat keras yang membaca sensor, mengontrol relay, dan berkomunikasi dengan server backend\cb1 \
\ls2\ilvl0
\f0 \cf2 \cb3 \kerning1\expnd0\expndtw0 \outl0\strokewidth0 {\listtext	2.	}\expnd0\expndtw0\kerning0
\outl0\strokewidth0 \strokec2 Google Apps Script (GAS) Backend
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4  \'97 Server middleware yang menyimpan data di Google Sheets, menangani autentikasi, dan menyediakan REST API\cb1 \
\ls2\ilvl0
\f0 \cf2 \cb3 \kerning1\expnd0\expndtw0 \outl0\strokewidth0 {\listtext	3.	}\expnd0\expndtw0\kerning0
\outl0\strokewidth0 \strokec2 Web Dashboard (PWA)
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4  \'97 Antarmuka pengguna berbasis web yang dapat di-install sebagai aplikasi mobile, untuk monitoring real-time dan kontrol perangkat\cb1 \
\pard\pardeftab720\sl560\sa240\partightenfactor0

\f2 \'a9\'b8\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'bc

\pard\pardeftab720\sl380\partightenfactor0
\cf6 \cb5 ### Alur Data\cb1 \
\
\cb5 1. **ESP32 membaca sensor** (INA219, ADS1115, ACS712, SHT31, PIR) setiap 5 detik\cb1 \
\cb5 2. **ESP32 upload data** ke GAS Backend setiap 60 detik via HTTPS POST\cb1 \
\cb5 3. **ESP32 long-poll** ke GAS Backend setiap 12 detik untuk menerima perintah\cb1 \
\cb5 4. **GAS menyimpan data** di Google Sheets (sensor_data, relay_status, event_log)\cb1 \
\cb5 5. **Dashboard** mengambil data dari GAS Backend saat dibuka\cb1 \
\cb5 6. **Dashboard** mengirim perintah kontrol relay/PWM ke GAS Backend\cb1 \
\cb5 7. **ESP32 menerima perintah** melalui long-poll dan mengeksekusi kontrol hardware\cb1 \
\
\cb5 ---\cb1 \
\
\cb5 ## 3. Komponen Perangkat Keras (Hardware)\cb1 \
\
\cb5 ### Daftar Komponen\cb1 \
\
\cb5 | Komponen | Jumlah | Fungsi |\cb1 \
\cb5 |----------|--------|--------|\cb1 \
\cb5 | ESP32 Dev Module | 1 | Mikrokontroler utama (240 MHz, 4MB Flash, 520KB SRAM) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | Panel Surya + MPPT | 1 | Pembangkit listrik tenaga surya |\cb1 \
\cb5 | Baterai LiFePO4 8S | 1 pack | Penyimpan energi (200Ah, 25.6V nominal) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | 74HC595 Shift Register | 4 buah | Ekspansi GPIO untuk 32 output relay |\cb1 \
\cb5 | Relay Module (Active-Low) | 13 unit | Saklar elektronik perangkat rumah tangga |\cb1 \
\cb5 | Solid State Relay / MOSFET | 1 unit | PV Disconnect (putus panel surya) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | INA219 | 1 | Sensor tegangan & arus DC output MPPT |\cb1 \
\cb5 | ADS1115 (16-bit ADC) | 2 | Monitoring tegangan 8 sel baterai individual |\cb1 \
\cb5 | ACS712-30A | 1 | Sensor arus AC beban rumah (RMS) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | SHT31 | 1 | Sensor suhu & kelembaban ruangan |\cb1 \
\cb5 | PIR HC-SR501 | 4 | Deteksi gerakan untuk otomasi pencahayaan |\cb1 \
\cb5 | LED (dengan driver PWM) | 1 | Lampu dimmable (Lampu Kamar Fatimah) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | MicroSD Card | 1 | Logging data sensor secara lokal |\cb1 \
\cb5 | Resistor Voltage Divider | 1 set | Pembagi tegangan untuk monitoring sel (360k\uc0\u937  + 10k\u937 ) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | Pull-up Resistor 4.7k\uc0\u937  | 4 | Pull-up I2C (SDA & SCL) |\cb1 \
\
\cb5 ### Wiring Diagram I2C\cb1 \
\
\
\

\f2 \'a9\'c0\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4
\f1  ADS1115 #1 (0x48)\
ESP32 GPIO22 (SCL) 
\f2 \'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'c8\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4\'a9\'a4

\f1  SHT31 (0x44)\
4.7k\uc0\u937  ke VCC pada masing-masing SDA & SCL\

\cf6 \cb5 ---\cb1 \
\
\cb5 ## 4. Pemetaan GPIO ESP32\cb1 \
\
\cb5 ### Tabel Pin GPIO Lengkap\cb1 \
\
\cb5 | GPIO | Mode | Fungsi | Keterangan |\cb1 \
\cb5 |------|------|--------|------------|\cb1 \
\cb5 | **2** | OUTPUT | Status LED | Built-in LED, indikator status sistem |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **4** | OUTPUT | PWM Channel 2 | LEDC PWM cadangan |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **5** | OUTPUT | SD Card CS | Chip Select SPI |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **12** | OUTPUT | PWM Channel 1 | LEDC PWM cadangan |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **13** | OUTPUT | PWM Channel 0 | Dimmer Lampu Kamar Fatimah |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **14** | OUTPUT | Shift Register DS | Serial Data Input 74HC595 |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **18** | OUTPUT | SD Card SCK | SPI Clock |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **19** | INPUT | SD Card MISO | Master In Slave Out |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **21** | I/O | I2C SDA | Data bus I2C (pull-up 4.7k\uc0\u937 ) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **22** | I/O | I2C SCL | Clock bus I2C (pull-up 4.7k\uc0\u937 ) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **23** | OUTPUT | SD Card MOSI | Master Out Slave In |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **25** | OUTPUT | Shift Register OE | Output Enable (ACTIVE LOW) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **26** | OUTPUT | Shift Register SH_CP | Shift Register Clock |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **27** | OUTPUT | Shift Register ST_CP | Storage Register Clock (Latch) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **33** | INPUT | ACS712 Output | Analog output sensor arus AC |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **34** | INPUT | PIR Sensor 1 | Hanya input (no pull-up) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **35** | INPUT | PIR Sensor 2 | Hanya input (no pull-up) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **36** (VP) | INPUT | PIR Sensor 3 | Hanya input (no pull-up) |\cb1 \
\cb5 | **39** (VN) | INPUT | PIR Sensor 4 | Hanya input (no pull-up) |\cb1 \
\
\cb5 ### Perhatian Penting\cb1 \
\
\cb5 - **GPIO 34, 35, 36, 39** hanya dapat digunakan sebagai **input** dan tidak memiliki pull-up/pull-down internal. Pin PIR harus menggunakan resistor pull-up eksternal atau mengandalkan pull-up modul PIR.\cb1 \
\cb5 - **GPIO 12** memiliki perilaku boot-strapping \'97 pastikan tidak dalam keadaan LOW saat boot agar ESP32 masuk mode flash normal.\cb1 \
\cb5 - **Shift Register OE (GPIO 25)** dibiarkan HIGH saat boot (semua relay OFF) untuk keselamatan. OE baru diaktifkan setelah inisialisasi selesai (safety delay 2 detik).\cb1 \
\
\cb5 ---\cb1 \
\

\cf6 \cb5 ---\cb1 \
\
\cb5 ## 6. Instalasi & Setup\cb1 \
\
\cb5 ### 6.1 Google Apps Script Backend\cb1 \
\
\cb5 #### Prasyarat\cb1 \
\
\cb5 - Akun Google (Gmail)\cb1 \
\cb5 - Google Sheets (Spreadsheet baru)\cb1 \
\cb5 - Google Apps Script (script.google.com)\cb1 \
\
\cb5 #### Langkah Setup\cb1 \
\
\cb5 1. **Buat Google Spreadsheet baru** di Google Sheets. Buat sheet-sheet (tab) berikut dengan header kolom persis seperti di bawah:\cb1 \
\
\cb5    | Nama Sheet | Header Kolom |\cb1 \
\cb5    |-----------|--------------|\cb1 \
\cb5    | `sensor_data` | timestamp, v_mppt, i_mppt, p_mppt, v_pack, soc_pct, temp, humi, v_cell1-v_cell8, i_ac, p_ac, pir1-pir4, relay_states, pwm_values, pv_connected |\cb1 \
\cb5    | `relay_status` | timestamp, relay_id, state, commanded_by, commanded_at |\cb1 \
\cb5    | `config` | key, value, updated_by, updated_at |\cb1 \
\cb5    | `automation_rules` | id, name, trigger_type, trigger_params, conditions_logic, conditions, actions, timeout_sec, enabled, priority, created_at, updated_at |\cb1 \
\cb5    | `event_log` | timestamp, event_type, severity, message, source, details |\cb1 \
\cb5    | `user_db` | username, password_hash, role, active, created_at, last_login, created_by |\cb1 \
\cb5    | `session_db` | token, username, role, created_at, expires_at, ip_address, user_agent |\cb1 \
\
\cb5 2. **Buka Google Apps Script** 
\f3 \uc0\u8594 
\f4  Extensions 
\f3 \uc0\u8594 
\f4  Apps Script (dari Spreadsheet)  \cb1 \
\cb5    Atau buka script.google.com 
\f3 \uc0\u8594 
\f4  New Project\cb1 \
\
\cb5 3. **Copy semua file .gs** dari folder `google-apps-script/` ke project GAS. Buat file baru untuk masing-masing:\cb1 \
\cb5    - `Code.gs` \'97 paste isi file\cb1 \
\cb5    - `Config_.gs` \'97 paste isi file\cb1 \
\cb5    - `Auth.gs` \'97 paste isi file\cb1 \
\cb5    - `Database.gs` \'97 paste isi file\cb1 \
\cb5    - `SensorData.gs` \'97 paste isi file\cb1 \
\cb5    - `RelayCommands.gs` \'97 paste isi file\cb1 \
\cb5    - `RulesEngine.gs` \'97 paste isi file\cb1 \
\cb5    - `PIRConfig.gs` \'97 paste isi file\cb1 \
\cb5    - `UserManager.gs` \'97 paste isi file\cb1 \
\cb5    - `EventLog.gs` \'97 paste isi file\cb1 \
\
\cb5 4. **Konfigurasi Config_.gs**:\cb1 \
\cb5    ```javascript\cb1 \
\cb5    var SPREADSHEET_ID = 'PASTE_SPREADSHEET_ID_ANDA_DISINI';\cb1 \
\cb5    var JWT_SECRET = 'BUAT_STRING_RANDOM_MINIMAL_32_KARAKTER';\cb1 \
\cb5    var DEVICE_API_KEY = 'BUAT_API_KEY_RANDOM_UNTUK_ESP32';\cb1 \
\
\

\f0\fs36 \cf2 \cb3 \strokec2 Perhitungan SOC\
\pard\pardeftab720\sa240\partightenfactor0

\f1\fs32 \cf4 \strokec4 SOC dihitung menggunakan aproksimasi linear berdasarkan tegangan pack:\
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \cb5 text\cb1 \
\pard\pardeftab720\qc\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0

\fs28 \cf6 \strokec6 \
\pard\pardeftab720\sl380\partightenfactor0

\f4 \cf6 \cb5 SOC (%) = ((V_pack - V_min) / (V_max - V_min)) \'d7 100\cb1 \
\
\cb5 Contoh:\cb1 \
\cb5   V_pack = 26.4V\cb1 \
\cb5   SOC = ((26.4 - 20.0) / (29.2 - 20.0)) \'d7 100\cb1 \
\cb5   SOC = (6.4 / 9.2) \'d7 100 = 69.6%\cb1 \
\
\
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0

\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \cb3 \
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0
\cf2 \cb1 \strokec2 \
\pard\pardeftab720\sa240\partightenfactor0

\f0 \cf2 \cb3 Catatan:
\f1  Metode ini bersifat estimasi. Untuk akurasi yang lebih tinggi, dapat ditambahkan Coulomb Counting di firmware versi mendatang.\cb1 \
\pard\pardeftab720\sa480\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \cb3 \strokec4 \
\pard\pardeftab720\sl500\sa240\partightenfactor0

\f0\fs38 \cf2 \strokec2 11. Sistem Kontrol Relay\
\pard\pardeftab720\sl560\sa240\partightenfactor0

\fs36 \cf2 Konfigurasi 74HC595 Shift Register\
\pard\pardeftab720\sa240\partightenfactor0

\f1\fs32 \cf4 \strokec4 4 buah IC 74HC595 daisy-chained menyediakan 32-bit output digital:\
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \cb5 text\cb1 \
\pard\pardeftab720\qc\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0

\fs28 \cf6 \strokec6 \
\pard\pardeftab720\sl380\partightenfactor0

\f4 \cf6 \cb5            Register 1 (bit 0-7)\cb1 \
\cb5            
\f3 \uc0\u9484 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9488 
\f4 \cb1 \
\cb5   Data 
\f3 \uc0\u9472 \u9472 \u9658 \u9474 
\f4  Q0 Q1 Q2 Q3 Q4 Q5 Q6 Q7
\f3 \uc0\u9474 \u9472 \u9472 
\f4  Relay 1-8\cb1 \
\cb5            
\f3 \uc0\u9492 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9496 
\f4 \cb1 \
\cb5                         
\f3 \uc0\u9474 
\f4  Serial Out\cb1 \
\cb5            Register 2 (bit 8-15)\cb1 \
\cb5            
\f3 \uc0\u9484 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9488 
\f4 \cb1 \
\cb5            
\f3 \uc0\u9474 
\f4  Q0 Q1 Q2 Q3 Q4 Q5 Q6 Q7
\f3 \uc0\u9474 \u9472 \u9472 
\f4  Relay 9-13, PV Disconnect\cb1 \
\cb5            
\f3 \uc0\u9492 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9472 \u9496 
\f4       (bit 13 = PV)\cb1 \
\cb5                         
\f3 \uc0\u9474 
\f4 \cb1 \

\f3 \uc0\u8592 
\f4  Cadangan ekspansi\cb1 \

\f3 \uc0\u8592 
\f4  Cadangan ekspansi\cb1 \
\

\f0\fs36 \cf2 \cb3 \strokec2 Sifat Relay Active-LOW\
\pard\pardeftab720\sa240\partightenfactor0

\f1\fs32 \cf4 \strokec4 Semua relay menggunakan konfigurasi 
\f0 \cf2 \strokec2 active-LOW
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4 , artinya:\
\pard\tx220\tx720\pardeftab720\li720\fi-720\sa160\partightenfactor0
\ls17\ilvl0
\f0 \cf2 \kerning1\expnd0\expndtw0 \outl0\strokewidth0 {\listtext	\uc0\u8226 	}\expnd0\expndtw0\kerning0
\outl0\strokewidth0 \strokec2 Bit 1
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4  di shift register \uc0\u8594  relay 
\f0 \cf2 \strokec2 ON
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4  ( energi )\cb1 \
\ls17\ilvl0
\f0 \cf2 \cb3 \kerning1\expnd0\expndtw0 \outl0\strokewidth0 {\listtext	\uc0\u8226 	}\expnd0\expndtw0\kerning0
\outl0\strokewidth0 \strokec2 Bit 0
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4  di shift register \uc0\u8594  relay 
\f0 \cf2 \strokec2 OFF
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4  ( aman )\cb1 \
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \cb3 \
\pard\pardeftab720\sa240\partightenfactor0
\cf4 Firmware secara otomatis melakukan 
\f0 \cf2 \strokec2 bit inversion
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4  sebelum mengirim ke shift register.\
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \
\pard\pardeftab720\sl560\sa240\partightenfactor0

\f0\fs36 \cf2 \strokec2 Safety Mechanism\
\pard\tx220\tx720\pardeftab720\li720\fi-720\sa160\partightenfactor0
\ls18\ilvl0
\fs32 \cf2 \kerning1\expnd0\expndtw0 \outl0\strokewidth0 {\listtext	1.	}\expnd0\expndtw0\kerning0
\outl0\strokewidth0 \strokec2 Boot Safety
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4 : GPIO OE (Output Enable) dibiarkan HIGH saat boot \uc0\u8594  semua relay OFF\cb1 \
\ls18\ilvl0
\f0 \cf2 \cb3 \kerning1\expnd0\expndtw0 \outl0\strokewidth0 {\listtext	2.	}\expnd0\expndtw0\kerning0
\outl0\strokewidth0 \strokec2 Safety Delay
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4 : Minimal 2 detik setelah boot sebelum relay diaktifkan\cb1 \
\ls18\ilvl0
\f0 \cf2 \cb3 \kerning1\expnd0\expndtw0 \outl0\strokewidth0 {\listtext	3.	}\expnd0\expndtw0\kerning0
\outl0\strokewidth0 \strokec2 PV Disconnect
\f1 \cf4 \strokec4 : Relay #14 secara independen memutus panel surya dari sistem\cb1 \
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \cb3 \

\f0\fs38 \cf2 \strokec2 12. Sistem Otomasi (Rules Engine)\
\pard\pardeftab720\sl560\sa240\partightenfactor0

\fs36 \cf2 Konsep\
\pard\pardeftab720\sa240\partightenfactor0

\f1\fs32 \cf4 \strokec4 Rules engine memungkinkan pembuatan aturan otomasi berdasarkan kondisi sensor. Rules dapat dibuat dari dashboard web dan dievaluasi secara lokal di ESP32 serta di server GAS.\
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \
\pard\pardeftab720\sl560\sa240\partightenfactor0

\f0\fs36 \cf2 \strokec2 Struktur Rule\
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0

\f1\fs32 \cf4 \cb5 \strokec4 text\cb1 \
\pard\pardeftab720\qc\partightenfactor0
\cf4 \
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0

\fs28 \cf6 \strokec6 \
\pard\pardeftab720\sl380\partightenfactor0

\f4 \cf6 \cb5 Rule \{\cb1 \
\cb5   id            : string    // ID unik (UUID)\cb1 \
\cb5   name          : string    // Nama deskriptif\cb1 \
\cb5   trigger_type  : string    // "time", "batt", "temp", "humi", "pir", "pv_i", "ac_i", "manual"\cb1 \
\cb5   conditions_logic: string  // "AND" atau "OR"\cb1 \
\cb5   conditions[]  : [\cb1 \
\cb5     \{ sensor_id: "soc_pct", op: "<", value: 20 \}    // contoh: SOC < 20%\cb1 \
\cb5     \{ sensor_id: "temp",    op: ">", value: 35 \}    // contoh: Suhu > 35\'b0C\cb1 \
\cb5   ]\cb1 \
\cb5   actions[]     : [\cb1 \
\cb5     \{ type: "relay_off", target: 13, value: 0 \}     // contoh: Matikan AC\cb1 \
\cb5     \{ type: "pwm_set",   target: 0, value: 50 \}     // contoh: PWM channel 0 
\f3 \uc0\u8594 
\f4  50%\cb1 \
\cb5     \{ type: "notification", message: "Baterai rendah!" \}\cb1 \
\cb5   ]\cb1 \
\cb5   timeout_sec   : int       // Timeout aksi (0 = permanen)\cb1 \
\cb5   enabled       : boolean   // Aktif/nonaktif\cb1 \
\cb5   priority      : int       // Prioritas (lebih tinggi = diproses dulu)\cb1 \
\cb5 \}\cb1 \
\
\
\pard\pardeftab720\partightenfactor0

\cb5 THEN relay_off(13), relay_off(10), notification("Baterai rendah! Beban berat dimatikan.")\cb1 \
\cb5 PRIORITY: 10\cb1 \
\cb5 TIMEOUT: 0 (permanen sampai SOC kembali normal)\cb1 \
\
